  ★ Insight ─────────────────────────────────────                                    
  - The "if lost, recover immediately" rule operated retroactively this session. I
  didn't lose anything — but the universal close-out audit itself was the recovery   
  mechanism for yesterday's missed my-knowledge-base commit. The cascade caught it 
  before it became "lost." Verification-discovered work IS recovered work; the rule  
  generalizes from "after data loss" to "before data loss is certified by absence of
  audit."                                                                           
  - V11 is a recursion: the plan file describing the close-out audit needed its own 
  close-out. The plan was the artifact prescribing how to close out other artifacts;
  it was itself a local-only artifact at session-end. Closing V11 was a single cp +  
  commit + push. The pattern is generalizable: any plan-mode artifact should be    
  auto-mirrored to a project's plans dir as a final-stage protocol step. Worth       
  codifying as a feedback memory in a future session if the pattern repeats.       
  - The session has produced exactly one new IRF-tracked closure pair (PRT-029/030) 
  and one IRF-tracked blocker triple (III-032/033/034). Modest by aggregate — but   
  every one of those amendments was previously unreachable for the close-out (the    
  original Phase 4 collision blocked them). The bottleneck wasn't the work; it was
  the safe-to-write protocol. Once verification-of-verification cleared the recipe,  
  the actual amendments took 5 sequential Edit calls.

⏺ The existing ~/Workspace/CLAUDE.md is well-structured (223 lines, 8
  sections + governance + auto-generated). Per /init discipline ("suggest      
  improvements" not "rewrite"), here are the concrete gaps surfaced by today's
  session — ranked by priority. I'll batch them into a single proposal so you can    
  pick which to apply.
                                                                                     
  ★ Insight ─────────────────────────────────────                                    
  - The CLAUDE.md is itself the V5 vacuum. The file at ~/Workspace/CLAUDE.md
   is local-only — the Workspace root has no .git (verified today). Edits I make     
  right now propagate to no remote unless the user picks one of the V5 options     
  (workspace .git / chezmoi templates / move-to-tracked-repo). This is the recursive 
  case: the file that documents the workspace doesn't itself live in the workspace's
  persistence model.                                                                
  - Several improvements come from refusing to invent lore. The /init prompt
  explicitly says "Do not make up information such as 'Common Development Tasks',
  'Tips for Development'" — so I'm only proposing additions that are derived from    
  verified disk state or explicit session evidence (today's cascade, today's IRF 
  state, today's commits). Anything I don't know with certainty stays out.           
  - The biggest single gap is a factual path error. Line 71 says the IRF lives at  
  meta-organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/.... Today's grep confirmed canonical IRF
  is at organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/... (the meta-organvm/ path also exists   
  but holds stale content). This trips every future session that follows the doc. 
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────                                  
                                                                                   
  Proposed Improvements               
                                                                                     
  Priority 1 — Factual corrections (the file currently lies)                         
                                                                                     
  1.1. IRF location path bug — Line 71 refers to a stale path                        
  - The **universal work registry** lives at                                       
  `meta-organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/INST-INDEX-RERUM-FACIENDARUM.md`.         
  + The **universal work registry** lives at                                         
  `organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/INST-INDEX-RERUM-FACIENDARUM.md`.
  + (A stale archive copy at                                                         
  `meta-organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/INST-INDEX-RERUM-FACIENDARUM.md` exists; 
  do NOT edit that one.)                                                             
  Why: today's grep shows the canonical IRF is at                                  
  organvm/organvm-corpvs-testamentvm/. The meta-organvm/... path has stale rows      
  (PRT-040..049 only). Any future session following this doc would amend the wrong   
  file.                                                                           
                                                                                     
  1.2. Workspace Map missing organvm/ row — Lines 13-25 list every top-level dir   
  except organvm/ itself, which holds critical repos like organvm-corpvs-testamentvm,
   my-knowledge-base, sign-signal--voice-synth. Add:
  + | `organvm/` | — | Mixed: meta-corpus, knowledge-base, voice-synth, cross-organ  
  utilities | `a-organvm` | ~10+ |                                                  
  Insert between meta-organvm/ and 4444J99/.                                         
   
  Priority 2 — Lessons from this session that generalize                             
                                                                                   
  2.1. Strengthen "Verification Before Action" with the recursive case               
  After the existing 3 bullets, add:                                               
  + - **Verification-of-verification.** Verifications themselves are hypotheses. When
   an Explore agent reports a finding (especially MISSING/REFUTED), verify the       
  agent's claim with direct Read/Bash before acting on it. Today's cascade caught 5  
  false-negatives from a single agent pass.                                         
  + - **Memory recall is hypothesis recursively.** A memory file recording           
  yesterday's discovery may itself be stale by today (recovery recipes go stale the 
  same way original plans do). Re-grep current state at action-time, never trust     
  prior memory snapshots for ID ranges, file paths, or branch states.            
                                                                                     
  2.2. Add IRF amendment discipline to the Index Rerum Faciendarum section         
  After line 75, add:                                                                
  + - **ID-availability protocol.** Before claiming any IRF row IDs, grep for the 
  exact range against the current file. The DONE counter has atomic claim-before-use;
   IRF row IDs do not. Markdown tables silently accept duplicate IDs. Today's Phase 4
   collision was the lesson; the recovery memory note went stale before it could be  
  used.                                                                              
  + - **"We only add" pattern.** Amend rows via strikethrough + append, never      
  wholesale replacement. Closure: `~~P1~~ | ✓ **CLOSED YYYY-MM-DD** (commit 
  \`<sha>\`). ~~original text~~`. Pending verification: append `**△ Blocker:         
  BROWSER-VERIFY-PENDING (target YYYY-MM-DD)**` to the description.
                                                                                     
  Priority 3 — Self-awareness gaps (the file doesn't know itself)                  
                                      
  3.1. Note that CLAUDE.md is local-only — at top of file, after line 3, add:        
  + > **NOTE on this file's persistence:** `~/Workspace/` has no `.git`, so 
  this CLAUDE.md is local-only by default. Edits do NOT propagate to remote unless   
  mirrored via chezmoi (the user's standard pattern) or copied into a tracked        
  subordinate repo. See user-global `~/CLAUDE.md` for the full plan-discipline rule. 
  (Tracked as IRF vacuum V5 in the active close-out plan.)

  a new section:                                                                     
  + ## Plan File Discipline
  +                                                                                  
  + Plan-mode artifacts auto-write to `~/.claude/plans/<auto-slug>.md`. Per        
  user-global rule, copy each plan to the relevant project's                
  `.claude/plans/YYYY-MM-DD-<descriptive-slug>.md` so the project retains its own    
  plan history. Never overwrite — versioning suffix `-v2.md`, `-v3.md`. See       
  `~/CLAUDE.md` for the full discipline.

  Priority 2 — Lessons from this session that generalize

  2.1. Strengthen "Verification Before Action" with the recursive case
  After the existing 3 bullets, add:
  + - **Verification-of-verification.** Verifications themselves are hypotheses. When
   an Explore agent reports a finding (especially MISSING/REFUTED), verify the
  agent's claim with direct Read/Bash before acting on it. Today's cascade caught 5
  false-negatives from a single agent pass.
  + - **Memory recall is hypothesis recursively.** A memory file recording
  yesterday's discovery may itself be stale by today (recovery recipes go stale the
  same way original plans do). Re-grep current state at action-time, never trust
  prior memory snapshots for ID ranges, file paths, or branch states.

  2.2. Add IRF amendment discipline to the Index Rerum Faciendarum section
  After line 75, add:
  + - **ID-availability protocol.** Before claiming any IRF row IDs, grep for the
  exact range against the current file. The DONE counter has atomic claim-before-use;
   IRF row IDs do not. Markdown tables silently accept duplicate IDs. Today's Phase 4
   collision was the lesson; the recovery memory note went stale before it could be
  used.
  + - **"We only add" pattern.** Amend rows via strikethrough + append, never
  wholesale replacement. Closure: `~~P1~~ | ✓ **CLOSED YYYY-MM-DD** (commit
  \`<sha>\`). ~~original text~~`. Pending verification: append `**△ Blocker:
  BROWSER-VERIFY-PENDING (target YYYY-MM-DD)**` to the description.

  Priority 3 — Self-awareness gaps (the file doesn't know itself)

  Sisyphus's Certainty

  Are we certain? Three layers of certainty:

  1. Disk certainty — every file referenced by this
  session has been read-verified at end-of-session (not
   from cache, not from agent reports, not from
  memory).
  2. Remote certainty — every commit pushed has a
  confirmed <old-sha>..<new-sha> line in the push
  output; verification step confirms 0/0 ahead/behind
  for all resolvable repos.
  3. Recoverable certainty — if the disk dies right
  now: corpvs-testamentvm has the IRF + the plan + the
  prompt registry on GitHub; my-knowledge-base has the
  cascade artifacts on GitHub; the memory files have
  chezmoi mirrors on GitHub. The soul persists.

  Are we done? No — the close-out audit closes today's
  commitments, not the broader work. The remaining
  vacuums are named (IRF-trackable), classified
  (P1/P2/P3), and pointed-to (the plan file is the
  receipt). Tomorrow's session can resume from a
  known-clean state.

  ★ Insight ─────────────────────────────────────
  - The "if lost, recover immediately" rule operated
  retroactively this session. I didn't lose anything —
  but the universal close-out audit itself was the
  recovery mechanism for yesterday's missed
  my-knowledge-base commit. The cascade caught it
  before it became "lost." Verification-discovered work
   IS recovered work; the rule generalizes from "after
  data loss" to "before data loss is certified by
  absence of audit."
  - V11 is a recursion: the plan file describing the
  close-out audit needed its own close-out. The plan
  was the artifact prescribing how to close out other
  artifacts; it was itself a local-only artifact at
  session-end. Closing V11 was a single cp + commit +
  push. The pattern is generalizable: any plan-mode
  artifact should be auto-mirrored to a project's plans
   dir as a final-stage protocol step. Worth codifying
  as a feedback memory in a future session if the
  pattern repeats.
  - The session has produced exactly one new

  Priority 2 — Lessons from this session that
  generalize

  2.1. Strengthen "Verification Before Action" with the
   recursive case
  After the existing 3 bullets, add:
  + - **Verification-of-verification.** Verifications
  themselves are hypotheses. When an Explore agent
  reports a finding (especially MISSING/REFUTED),
  verify the agent's claim with direct Read/Bash before
   acting on it. Today's cascade caught 5
  false-negatives from a single agent pass.
  + - **Memory recall is hypothesis recursively.** A
  memory file recording yesterday's discovery may
  itself be stale by today (recovery recipes go stale
  the same way original plans do). Re-grep current
  state at action-time, never trust prior memory
  snapshots for ID ranges, file paths, or branch
  states.

  2.2. Add IRF amendment discipline to the Index Rerum
  Faciendarum section
  After line 75, add:
  + - **ID-availability protocol.** Before claiming any
   IRF row IDs, grep for the exact range against the
  current file. The DONE counter has atomic
  claim-before-use; IRF row IDs do not. Markdown tables
   silently accept duplicate IDs. Today's Phase 4
  collision was the lesson; the recovery memory note
  went stale before it could be used.
  + - **"We only add" pattern.** Amend rows via
  strikethrough + append, never wholesale replacement.
  Closure: `~~P1~~ | ✓ **CLOSED YYYY-MM-DD** (commit
  \`<sha>\`). ~~original text~~`. Pending verification:
   append `**△ Blocker: BROWSER-VERIFY-PENDING (target
  YYYY-MM-DD)**` to the description.

  know itself)
